üìú Singularity of Purpose Statement (Click to expand) ‚ñº
‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó ‚ïë THE SINGULARITY OF PURPOSE ‚ïë ‚ï†‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ï£ ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë MCI exists for ONE reason: ‚ïë ‚ïë To give the operator VISIBILITY and CONTROL over CIA-SIE-PURE. ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë MCI provides: ‚ïë ‚ïë 1. A way to AUTHENTICATE (Token Capture) ‚ïë ‚ïë 2. A way to VERIFY readiness (Pre-Ignition Scan) ‚ïë ‚ïë 3. A way to START safely (Ignition) ‚ïë ‚ïë 4. A way to SEE what's happening (Telemetry) ‚ïë ‚ïë 5. A way to STOP safely (Shutdown) ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë MCI does NOT provide: ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Trading algorithms ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Order execution ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Position management ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Broker connections ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Data storage ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë Those are the ENGINE's job. MCI is the COCKPIT. ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë WITHOUT MCI: Operator is BLIND. ‚ïë ‚ïë WITH MCI: Operator can SEE, CONTROL, and RESPOND. ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù
‚öñÔ∏è Clean Slate Protocol Interpretation (Click to expand) ‚ñº
‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó ‚ïë CLEAN SLATE = SUPERSESSION OF DESIGN, NOT DESTRUCTION OF CODE ‚ïë ‚ï†‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ï£ ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë The Clean Slate Protocol was declared BEFORE the code was audited. ‚ïë ‚ïë The assumption was: previous code doesn't match the specification. ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë The audit PROVED: previous code ALREADY matches the specification. ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë THEREFORE: ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ The DESIGN intent of Clean Slate is satisfied ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ The code aligns with that design ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Deleting code that already works serves no purpose ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚Ä¢ Rebuilding identical code introduces regression risk ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë RECOMMENDATION: RETROFIT, not FRESH BUILD ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïë ‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù

Q What is the SINGULAR PURPOSE of MCI? ‚ñº
MCI exists for ONE purpose: To MONITOR and CONTROL the CIA-SIE-PURE trading engine. It is the COCKPIT, not the ENGINE. Like a car dashboard: ‚Ä¢ Dashboard shows speed, fuel, temperature (MCI) ‚Ä¢ Engine moves the car (CIA-SIE-PURE) ‚Ä¢ Dashboard cannot drive - it can only START/STOP and MONITOR MCI does NOT trade. MCI does NOT execute. MCI WATCHES and CONTROLS. This is the SINGULARITY OF PURPOSE - everything MCI does serves this one goal.
singularity purpose identity fundamental
2026-01-24 ‚Ä¢ Core Identity

Q How should the CLEAN SLATE PROTOCOL be interpreted? ‚ñº
CLEAN SLATE PROTOCOL - CORRECT INTERPRETATION: What Clean Slate MEANS: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚úì Previous DESIGN decisions are superseded by new specifications ‚úì New Use Case Specification is the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH ‚úì Any code that VIOLATES the specification should be removed ‚úì Fresh perspective on requirements and architecture What Clean Slate does NOT MEAN: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚úó Delete all existing code blindly ‚úó Ignore good work already done ‚úó Rebuild things that already work ‚úó Destroy compliant implementations THE PRAGMATIC INTERPRETATION: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ "Clean Slate" applies to DESIGN THINKING, not CODE DESTRUCTION. If existing code ALIGNS with the new specification ‚Üí RETAIN If existing code VIOLATES the new specification ‚Üí REMOVE/REDO Current code ALIGNS with specifications (97% compliance). Therefore: RETROFIT, not demolition.
clean-slate interpretation protocol

Q What are the 5 PHASES of MCI operation? ‚ñº
THE 5 OPERATIONAL PHASES OF MCI: PHASE 0: TOKEN CAPTURE ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ User logs into Kite ‚Ä¢ Captures authentication token ‚Ä¢ Token stored securely ‚Ä¢ Expiry set for 6:00 AM IST next day ‚Ä¢ CR-004 governs this phase PHASE 1: PRE-IGNITION SCAN ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ 12-point system check (NSE/BSE) ‚Ä¢ Validate market hours ‚Ä¢ Check broker connectivity ‚Ä¢ Verify token validity ‚Ä¢ All systems GO/NO-GO status PHASE 2: IGNITION ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ Select backend (Zerodha, ICICI, HDFC, Kotak) ‚Ä¢ Two-stage safety (ARM ‚Üí IGNITE) ‚Ä¢ Send START signal to CIA-SIE-PURE ‚Ä¢ Engine begins trading operations PHASE 3: RUNNING (TELEMETRY) ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ Real-time position monitoring ‚Ä¢ P&L tracking ‚Ä¢ WebSocket telemetry stream ‚Ä¢ Dashboard displays all metrics ‚Ä¢ MCI WATCHES but does NOT trade PHASE 4: SHUTDOWN ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ Two-stage safety (ARM ‚Üí SHUTDOWN) ‚Ä¢ 6-step graceful sequence (CR-002) ‚Ä¢ All positions handled by ENGINE ‚Ä¢ MCI sends STOP signal only ‚Ä¢ Clean exit with logging Flow: 0 ‚Üí 1 ‚Üí 2 ‚Üí 3 ‚Üí 4 ‚Üí (back to 0 next day)
phases operation lifecycle

Q What is the 7-LAYER REVIEW for understanding solidification? ‚ñº
THE 7-LAYER REVIEW - SINGULARITY OF PURPOSE: LAYER 1: FUNDAMENTAL TRUTH ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ CIA-SIE-PURE = ENGINE (Python, executes trades) MCI = COCKPIT (TypeScript, monitors & controls) They are SEPARATE. They COMMUNICATE via API. LAYER 2: ANALOGIES THAT STICK ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ Car: Dashboard (MCI) vs Engine (CIA-SIE-PURE) ‚Ä¢ Airplane: Cockpit (MCI) vs Jet Engines (CIA-SIE-PURE) ‚Ä¢ Hospital: Monitoring Station (MCI) vs Life Support (CIA-SIE-PURE) LAYER 3: THE 5 PHASES ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ Token ‚Üí Scan ‚Üí Ignition ‚Üí Running ‚Üí Shutdown LAYER 4: THE 5 CONSTITUTIONAL REQUIREMENTS ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ CR-001: Token Validity CR-002: Graceful Shutdown CR-003: WHAT/WHY/HOW Errors CR-004: 6:00 AM IST Expiry CR-005: UXMI 7-State Components LAYER 5: AUDIT VERDICT ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ 97% quality, 5/5 CR compliance, 3 cosmetic fixes only LAYER 6: THE DECISION ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ RETROFIT (not Fresh Build) Clean Slate = Design supersession, not code destruction LAYER 7: SINGULAR PURPOSE ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ MCI exists to MONITOR and CONTROL. Nothing more. Nothing less. Every feature, every component, every line of code serves this ONE purpose.

Q How does the Session Checkpoint System work? ‚ñº
SESSION CHECKPOINT SYSTEM - CONTINUITY PROTOCOL: PURPOSE: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ Preserve session state across Claude Code sessions. Enable "rehydration" - resuming work without context loss. Track milestones and progress over time. KEY COMPONENTS: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ 1. MASTER_CONTEXT.md ‚Ä¢ Living document updated each session ‚Ä¢ Contains: CRs, QGs, checkpoint log, project state ‚Ä¢ Location: _SESSION_CHECKPOINTS/ 2. Session Archives ‚Ä¢ Snapshot of each significant session ‚Ä¢ Named: SESSION_ARCHIVE_[DATE]_[MILESTONE].md ‚Ä¢ Contains: Work done, decisions made, outcomes 3. Checkpoint IDs ‚Ä¢ Format: MCI-CHKPT-[DATE]-[MILESTONE] ‚Ä¢ Examples: - MCI-CHKPT-2026-01-24-DOC-CLASS - MCI-CHKPT-2026-01-24-REORG - MCI-CHKPT-2026-01-24-USECASE REHYDRATION PROTOCOL: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ To resume any session: 1. Read: /Users/.../MASTER_CONTEXT.md 2. Say: "Continue MCI project. Last checkpoint: [checkpoint-id]" 3. Claude will have full context to continue This ensures no loss of understanding between sessions. Project continuity is maintained across context boundaries.

Q What is the Singularity of Purpose for MCI? ‚ñº
THE SINGULARITY OF PURPOSE: MCI exists for ONE reason: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ To give the operator VISIBILITY and CONTROL over CIA-SIE-PURE. MCI PROVIDES (The 5 Capabilities): ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ 1. A way to AUTHENTICATE (Token Capture) 2. A way to VERIFY readiness (Pre-Ignition Scan) 3. A way to START safely (Ignition) 4. A way to SEE what's happening (Telemetry) 5. A way to STOP safely (Shutdown) MCI DOES NOT PROVIDE: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ Trading algorithms ‚Ä¢ Order execution ‚Ä¢ Position management ‚Ä¢ Broker connections ‚Ä¢ Data storage Those are the ENGINE's job. MCI is the COCKPIT. THE LITMUS TEST: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ WITHOUT MCI: Operator is BLIND. WITH MCI: Operator can SEE, CONTROL, and RESPOND. That is the entire purpose. Nothing more. Nothing less.

Q How was the Clean Slate Protocol interpreted? ‚ñº
CLEAN SLATE PROTOCOL INTERPRETATION: ORIGINAL DECLARATION (Use Case Specification): "ALL PREVIOUS CODE TO BE ERADICATED" AUDIT FINDING: Current code is 97% compliant with the specification THE INTERPRETATION: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚ïî‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïó ‚ïë CLEAN SLATE = SUPERSESSION OF DESIGN, NOT DESTRUCTION OF CODE ‚ïë ‚ïö‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïù The Clean Slate Protocol was declared BEFORE the code was audited. The assumption was: previous code doesn't match the specification. The audit PROVED: previous code ALREADY matches the specification. THEREFORE: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ ‚Ä¢ The DESIGN intent of Clean Slate is satisfied ‚Ä¢ The code aligns with that design ‚Ä¢ Deleting code that already works serves no purpose ‚Ä¢ Rebuilding identical code introduces regression risk FINAL RECOMMENDATION: ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ‚îÅ RETROFIT, not FRESH BUILD ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê ‚îÇ Factor ‚îÇ Fresh Build ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ Winner ‚îÇ ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§ ‚îÇ Time ‚îÇ HIGH ‚îÇ LOW ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ ‚îÇ Risk ‚îÇ MEDIUM ‚îÇ LOW ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ ‚îÇ Quality ‚îÇ N/A ‚îÇ 97% ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ ‚îÇ CR Status ‚îÇ REBUILD ‚îÇ MET ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ ‚îÇ P2/P3 Work ‚îÇ REDO ‚îÇ DONE ‚îÇ Retrofit ‚îÇ ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¥‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¥‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¥‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò

Engineering Principle

SCHEMATIC-FIRST: No coding until Layer 2 (Architecture) is complete. Just as no circuit is built without a schematic, no code is written without flowcharts.

1. CLAUDE CODE

Anthropic CLI Development Environment
80% USAGE
Description: Claude Code is an agentic coding tool that operates directly in your terminal, understanding your codebase and helping you code faster through intelligent context, autonomous execution, and natural language commands.
‚úì CAPABILITIES
  • File read/write/edit operations
  • Bash command execution
  • Project-wide codebase understanding
  • Architecture design & documentation
  • Testing & debugging assistance
  • Git operations & version control
  • CR compliance verification
‚ö° PRIORITY USE CASES
  • Generating complete code implementations
  • Creating architecture flowcharts (Mermaid)
  • Writing documentation & specifications
  • Complex debugging & error resolution
  • Multi-file refactoring
  • Session archiving & context management

üìö INTERNATIONAL STANDARDS COMPLIANCE

This Tool Arsenal follows internationally recognized software engineering standards for tool selection, categorization, and lifecycle mapping:

ISO/IEC 12207:2017

Systems and Software Engineering ‚Äî Software Life Cycle Processes. Defines 43 processes organized into four process groups. Tool phases mapped accordingly.

IEEE 1074:2006

Standard for Developing a Software Project Life Cycle Process. Establishes the process groups and activities for software development lifecycle.

PMBOK 7th Edition

Project Management Body of Knowledge. Defines 8 performance domains and 12 project management principles for tool governance.

TOGAF 10

The Open Group Architecture Framework. Enterprise architecture methodology for tool selection and technology governance.
